 ) india today-karvi ke mood of da nesan july 2018 pole (MOTN, july 2018) ke mutabik bijepi ke saath-saath endie kii siten pichlalocabhachunaav kii tulana main kaaphi kam ho rahi he
 The biggest reason for the decrease in seats is believed to be the solidarity of the opposition parties
 bataa den ki yahsurvey97 sansadeey kshetron or 197 vidhansabha kshetron ke 12,100 logon ke bich karaayaa gaya
 The survey was conducted between 18 July 2018 and 29 July 2018
 india today-karvi ke mood of da nesan survey ke mutabik 543 loksabhaa siton main sebijapi ko 245 sitenmilti dikh rahi hai
 Whereas in the 2014 elections, it got 282 seats
 is tarah se pichley chunaav kii tulana main 37 siten ghatati dikh rahi hai
 In this way, BJP is getting 27 seats less than the majority figure of 272 seats on its own
 vahiin, survey ke mutabikcongress ko 83 siten milneka anumaan he
 Whereas in the last Lok Sabha election, 44 seats were won
 is tarah se congress ko 39 siton kaa ijapha hota dikh rahaa he
 Although far from the magical figure of the majority
 haalanki, 281 siten endie gathbandhan ko mil rahi hai
 At the same time, 122 seats can go to the UPA account, while the remaining 140 seats are expected to be in the account of other allies
 lekin sapa, basapa, tiemasi, tidipi or pidipi jaise dal agar upie ke saath milakar chunaav ladate hai to aise main nattejey chaunkaane vaale ho sakate hai
 In this case, NDA can get 255 seats and UPA can get 242 seats
 jabaki anya ko 46 siten mil sakati he
 BJP is most likely to lose seats in Uttar Pradesh, where BJP and its ally Apna Dal won 73 out of 80 parliamentary seats in the last Lok Sabha election
 haal ke dinon sapa-basapa ke ek saath aane se bijepi kaa siyaasi sameekaran gadabadaya he
 Recently, BJP has lost in the by-elections in three Lok Sabha seats of UP
 bijepi ko doosraa jhatka bihar se lagata dikh rahaa he
 In the last Lok Sabha election, the BJP had contested from Nitish Kumar in Bihar and the results were much better
 bihari kii kul 40 loksabhaa siten hai
 Of these, BJP got 22 and its allies LJP 6 and RLSP got 3 seats
 2015 ke vidhansabha chunaav se argedy kaa graph badha he
 Recently, RJD candidate won the by-election in Bihar
 argedy netaa tejasvi lagaataar bihar main sakriy hai
 The JDU is believed to have regrouped with the BJP, considering the number of seats it contested in the last election
 is baar ke chunaav main usase kam siton par ladegi
 In such a situation, it is natural to reduce seats
 bijepi kii siten kam hone vaale rajya main teesraa rajya maharashtra mana ja rahaa he
 In the state, Congress and NCP have indicated to contest elections together
 jabaki bijepi or shivasena donon ne alag-alag chunaav ladane kii baat kahi he
 In such a situation, the results of the last Lok Sabha elections in Maharashtra are difficult to replicate
 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav main rajasthan or gujarat kii sabhi siton par bijepi ne jeet darj kii thi
 In Rajasthan, the BJP has lost two of its Lok Sabha seats to the Congress in the by-elections
 aise main pichley chunaav ke nattejey doharaana kaaphi kathin he
 Similarly, in Gujarat also, the graph of Congress has increased in the assembly elections
 aise main congress kii siten bad sakati hai
 However, the BJP has focused on Odisha and West Bengal to make up for the losses in these states
 yahi vajah he ki in donon rajyon main bijepi lagaataar sakriy he
 But it is difficult to say that these two states can recover the loss caused in the rest of the state

 Sriram Properties Captain Amarinder Singh's government of Punjab has taken a step on a matter related to Dalits
 punjab sarkaar ne pisies-je (jeudicial) kii pariksha main anusuchit jati (essi varg) ke abhyarthiyon ko keval chaar maukey dene kaa faisla lagu kiya he
 Whereas before this, the rule of giving unlimited examination till the age limit prescribed for SC category was in force
 punjab sarkaar ne kendriya anusuchit ayog or rajya essi ayog ko jaankaree die bina hi pisies-je (jeudicial) main badlaav kiya he
 This decision of Capt Amarinder Singh Government has warmed up politics
 punjab ekta party ke adhyaksh sukhpal singh khera ne mukhyamantri ko patr likhakar faisla badalane ke liye kaha he
 Sukhpal Singh Khaira termed the decision taken by the government regarding the PCSJ (judicial) examination as a violation of the rights of students belonging to the SC category
 unhone kaha he ki rajya sarkaar ne gupachup tareeke se essi varg ke liye bani nitiyon main bada badlaav kar diya he
 Khaira has said, 'the entire decision has been taken illegally without the advice of the National Commission for Scheduled Castes and the Punjab SC Commission, while as per Article 338 (9) of the Constitution of India, for any major changes affecting the Dalits It is mandatory for the central and state governments to consult the National Commission for Schedule Castes
 unhone maang kii he ki rajya sarkaar dwaara anusuchit jati varg ke khilaaf liye gaye ukt faisle ko turant waapas liya jaae

 It will include candidates from all communities
 jabaki abhi tak anusuchit jati ke abhyarthiyon ke liye aseemit baar pariksha main baithne kii chhot thi
 Significantly, Punjab has the highest percentage of Dalits in India
